<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<ul><li> Some think that Wilhelm Rust, for whatever reason, withheld this from publication with the BGA. The manuscript was discovered in 1917. It is now Mus. Ms. Bach P. 968 of the Royal Library of Berlin.
</li></ul>
